</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="prevention-of-anaemia-in-pregnancy">Prevention of anaemia in pregnancy.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#prevention-of-anaemia-in-pregnancy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Anaemia in pregnancy can be prevented. This is best done in mch/fp when the woman comes for routine antenatal care services. The following measures measures are done:</p>
<ul>
<li>Pre-conceptional care services</li>
<li>All pregnant women to receive sp top prevent malaria.</li>
<li>All pregnant women to sleep under treated insecticides net.</li>
<li>All pregnant women to receive haematenics.</li>
<li>All pregnant women to receive mebendazole.</li>
<li>Advice on a balanced diet rich in iron</li>
<li>Avoid milk products which discourage absorption of iron.</li>
<li>Routine physical examination.</li>
<li>ANC profile</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="principles-of-management">Principles of management.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#principles-of-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Raise Hb.</li>
<li>Eradicate the cause.</li>
<li>Prevent complications. The mother can be managed as an outpatient.</li>
<li>Triage</li>
<li>Height and measurement</li>
</ul>
<p>This document is available on
5
studocu
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Take detailed history</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="e28c5a96">Management of mild anaemia – Hb 8 – 10.5g/dl<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#e28c5a96" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Perform physical examination</li>
<li>Antenatal profile</li>
<li>Advice on taking oral haematenics. Talk about compliance and factors hindering malabsorption.</li>
<li>Administer SP according to guidelines to prevent malaria which can aggravate anaemia.</li>
<li>Let the mother sleep under insecticide treated net to prevent her from mosquito bites hence prevent malaria.</li>
<li>Administer mebendazole to prevent hookworm infestation.</li>
<li>Eliminate cause of anaemia</li>
<li>Provide mother with health education on diet rich in vitamin C, ferrous folic acid and how to prepare meals.</li>
<li>Book her to the high risk clinic.</li>
<li>Increase the frequency of visits.</li>
<li>Advice on ANC attendance.</li>
<li>Re-check Hb on 4th visit.</li>
<li>Manage according to FANC.</li>
<li>Continue with antenatal follow up.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="management-of-severe-anaemia-hb-7g-dl">Management of severe anaemia Hb &lt; 7g/dl<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management-of-severe-anaemia-hb-7g-dl" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>If in a basic obstetric health care facility refer the mother to a comprehensive care facility.</li>
<li>Admit the mother to antenatal ward</li>
<li>Provide complete bed rest.</li>
<li>Maintain nutritional status</li>
<li>Establish intra venous access and take blood sample for grouping and cross match.</li>
</ul>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Prepare to transfuse mother with packed cell to avoid cardiac overload.</li>
<li>Monitor vital signs Control vitals i.e. TPRBP 4hourly + FHR.</li>
<li>Prop up mother if dipnoec and administer oxygen PRN.</li>
<li>Do daily P.E to detect abnormalities.</li>
<li>Transfuse with whole blood and monitor vitals during labour.</li>
<li>Administer antibiotics with evidence of infection.</li>
<li>Review lab results i.e. Bs for malaria.</li>
<li>In case the mother has malaria parasites treat the mother as a case of complicated malaria.</li>
<li>Identify cause and manage.</li>
<li>Assess Hb weekly.</li>
<li>Educate mother on the condition.</li>
<li>Observe for signs of labour.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="management-during-labour">Management during labour<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management-during-labour" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Admit.</li>
<li>Reassure the mother and relatives.</li>
<li>Take proper history.</li>
<li>Vital observations of maternal and fetal condition.</li>
<li>Perform physical examination.</li>
<li>Take blood sample for investigations.</li>
<li>Arrange for transfusion.</li>
<li>Monitor mother while on transfusion.</li>
<li>Monitor labour by use of partograph.</li>
<li>Augument labour with sintocinon 2.5 – 5 i.u. in 500mls of normal saline in case of poor uterine contractions</li>
<li>Let the mother adopt position of choice. Prop up position can be adopted if the mother is presenting with dyspnoa.</li>
<li>Administer oxygen by mask to improve saturations</li>
<li>Avoid cardiac overload</li>
<li>Second stage can be supported with assisted vaginal delivery – AVD</li>
</ul>
<p>This document is available on
5 studocu
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
<li>An episiotomy can be administered to shorten second stage of labour.</li>
<li>Anticipate an asphyxiated baby.</li>
<li>Strengthen active management of third stage.</li>
<li>Severe anaemia with congestive cardiac failure, avoid the use of ergometrine.</li>
<li>Administer sintocinon 20 i.u. in 500mls of normal saline as to prevent atonic uterus.</li>
<li>Encourage early breastfeeding to encourage uterine contractions</li>
<li>Oserve aseptic measures.</li>
<li>Counsel the mother nonfamily planning.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="postnatal">Postnatal<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#postnatal" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Encourage on follow up.</li>
<li>Encourage the mother to practice personal hygiene.</li>
<li>Encourage the mother to take a balanced diet rich in iron.</li>
<li>Let the mother continue with haematenics</li>
<li>Let the mother be counseled on family planning.</li>
<li>Address the cause of anemia and manage it.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="cardiac-disease-in-pregnancy">CARDIAC DISEASE IN PREGNANCY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cardiac-disease-in-pregnancy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>It refers to disorders that affect the heart muscles, valves or blood vessels.</p>
<p>Also referred to as impairment of the heart.</p>
<p>This condition impairs the ability of the heart to supply tissue with oxygen.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="predisposing-factors">Predisposing factors<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#predisposing-factors" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Anaemia</li>
<li>Smoking</li>
<li>Alcohol</li>
</ul>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="grade-1">Grade 1<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#grade-1" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The woman presets with no signs and symptoms of cardiac disease. The woman only has a foci.</p>
<p>The woman gets to know about the condition from the health worker upon routine physical examination at the clinic.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="grade-2">Grade 2<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#grade-2" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The woman presents with signs and symptoms of cardiac disease only after performing strenuous worker.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="grade-3">Grade 3<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#grade-3" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The woman presents with signs and symptoms of cardiac disease after just performing normal duties.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="grade-4">Grade 4<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#grade-4" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="effects-to-the-fetus">Effects to the fetus<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#effects-to-the-fetus" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="pre-conception-advice-and-care">Pre-conception advice and care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#pre-conception-advice-and-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Advice any woman with a known cardiac disease to seek medical advice from the cardiologist before conception.</p>
<p>Counseling on maternal and fetal risks should be done before conception. This allows the woman to make a choice for conception.</p>
<p>General health advice should be given by the midwife with regards to diet, weight, exercise, rest, prevention of anaemia, avoidance of tobacco alcohol and drugs.</p>
<p>Surgical intervention can be done by the cardiologist e.g. mitral valvotomy.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="antenatal-care">Antenatal care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#antenatal-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="aims">Aims<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#aims" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>☑ Maintain state of hemodynamic state</li>
<li>☑ Prevent complications</li>
<li>☑ minimize additional load</li>
<li>☑ monitor for deterioration</li>
<li>☑ Provide physical and psychological support</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="management-antenatally">Management antenatally<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management-antenatally" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Pregnant woman with heart disease should be managed in a comprehensive emergency obstetrical and newborn care facility.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Management is by multidisciplinary team.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Grade 1 and 2 of the heart disease can be managed in an outpatient and book for hospital delivery.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Let the mother be booked at high risk joint clinic run by a cardiologist and obstetrician every 2 weekly until 30 weeks gestation then weekly thereafter till delivery.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>On each visit grading of the disease is done.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Evaluate fetal condition during each visit.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Do an abdominal ultra sound to confirm gestational age and congenital abnormalities.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Assess for fetal growth and amniotic fluid volume</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Monitor fetal heart rate</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Teach the mother on fetal kick chart to rule out fetal compromise.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Advice the mother on adequate rest.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Counsel and monitor on weight gain.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Let the mother report any signs of infection early.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Advice on diet.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Handle any dental condition appropriately.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Prophylactic antibiotics in case of risk of endocarditis.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>include routine antenatal care management i.e.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>height and weight measurement</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>history taking</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>physical examination</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>antenatal profile</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>provision of insecticide treated net</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>administration of sp</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>administration of mebendazole</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>administration of ifas</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
<li>administration of tetanus toxoid</li>
<li>emtct</li>
<li>health education – ibp &amp; danger signs and her cardiac condition.</li>
<li>book for next visit – for the cardiac disease increase the frequency.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="management-during-first-stage-of-labour">Management during first stage of labour<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#management-during-first-stage-of-labour" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Admit the mother in a cardiac bed</li>
<li>Reassure the mother</li>
<li>Take proper history</li>
<li>Perform physical examination</li>
<li>Monitor labour by use of partograph</li>
<li>Manage pain</li>
<li>Observe infection prevention</li>
<li>Provide support</li>
<li>Breathe through the mouth during a contraction</li>
<li>Empty bladder 2 hourly and test urine</li>
<li>Administer antihypertensive</li>
<li>Administer diuretics</li>
<li>Prepare for second stage of labour</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="infection-prevention">INFECTION PREVENTION.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#infection-prevention" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Infection prevention is one of the key components in provision of care. Transmission of infection despite provision of skilled service in order to save life can be the cause of morbidity and mortality. <strong>REMEMBER</strong> sepsis is the second leading cause of maternal mortality worldwide.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="sources-of-infection-in-maternal-care">Sources of infection in maternal care.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sources-of-infection-in-maternal-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

<ul>
<li>Repeated vaginal examinations</li>
<li>Improper waste disposal</li>
<li>Dirty delivery couch</li>
<li>Improper cord care</li>
<li>Dirty baby care unit</li>
<li>Relatives</li>
<li>Not washing hands</li>
<li>Unsterilized equipments</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="ways-of-preventing-infection">Ways of preventing infection.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#ways-of-preventing-infection" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Hand washing with soap and water.</li>
</ol>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260119-ab360bc1.jpeg" alt="img-19.jpeg"></p>
<p>Hand washing is very key. It eliminates most of the micro organisms. Hand washing is a skill of which all health service providers should appreciate. Before attending to the next patient it is advisable one should be able to wash their hands with soap and water. Always follow the steps of proper hand washing. Hand scrub can be done in case of performing surgical operations.</p>
<p>NOTE - where a health service provider is using sanitizer instead of hand wash then after every four clients with the sanitizer hand washing should be done.</p>
<ol start="2">
<li>Aseptic technique</li>
<li>Proper waste segregation and disposal</li>
</ol>
<p>All waste should be disposed where it belongs. Use the following chart for more information.</p>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>

<ol start="4">
<li>High level disinfection and sterilization</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>High level disinfection</li>
</ul>
<p>This is the standard process where once equipments are used and contaminated they should undergo a process of preparation to make them sterile again.</p>
<p>Step one – Prepare three buckets for chlorine, soapy water and clean water</p>
<p>Step two – Reconstitute chlorine at 0.5 % concentration</p>
<p>Step three – Immense used equipments in chlorine for 10 minutes</p>
<p>Step four – Remove equipments from chlorine and dip equipments in soapy water.</p>
<p>Step five – Rinse equipments in clean water.</p>
<p>This document is available on</p>
<p>5</p>
<p>studocu</p>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260119-b0b16402.jpeg" alt="img-20.jpeg"></p>
<ul>
<li>Sterilization</li>
<li>Put the equipments in an autoclave</li>
<li>Plastic equipments are put in cidex for 20 minutes. Thereafter rinse with distilled water or normal saline and pack them in a sterile container.</li>
<li>Strenuous solution can be used.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>NOTE</strong>: all sterile equipments have a shelf life of 14 days.</p>
<ol start="5">
<li>Health education</li>
</ol>
<p>Teach the clients on infection prevention.</p>
